<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Strategic agreement with Sovcomflot to create a 
marine JV </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-
size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>CGG CEO, Jean-Georges Malcor, 
commented:
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman"><I>&laquo; Given the current weak market conditions 
characterized notably by the unpredictable capex spending of our clients, delays
in awarding
projects and pressure on prices, we anticipate 2014 to remain difficult. In this
context, CGG has decided to accelerate and intensify its restructuring measures 
into 2014, downsizing the fleet from 18 to 13 vessels by the end of the year and
disposing of its North America land acquisition business to Geokinetics. Thanks 
to the full commitment of our employees we managed to deliver resilient 
profitability this quarter. </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><I>We anticipate, with this new perimeter, a sequential improvement 
in our results during the second half of the year sustained by a typically 
strong fourth
quarter. The set of measures put in place during 2014 allow us to confirm our 
objective of 400 bps Ebit margin improvement in 2016.&raquo; </I></P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman"><B>Equipment division Total Revenue </B>was $196 
million, down 23% compared to the second quarter of 2013 and down 5%
sequentially. The weakness of the seismic acquisition market is translating into
lower seismic equipment spending. Nevertheless in this context, Sercel is 
increasing its market share. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">External sales were $148 million, down 21% and internal sales 
represented 24% of total revenue, down 27% as a consequence of the CGG&#146;s 
fleet downsizing.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman">In June, Sercel was awarded by Argas, our partner in the
Middle East, the 60 000 channel count crew in Saudi Arabia. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman">Interest for the 508<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-
align:top">XT</SUP> acquisition system among our clients is increasing. In 
addition to the first two
508<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">XT</SUP> systems being 
delivered to the industry in June, Sercel announced at the European seismic 
convention (EAGE) that a system had been sold to PanAmerican Geophysical for 
delivery in July and
will be deployed in North America. During this convention, Sercel also launched 
the new land vibrator &#147;Go Anywhere&#148; Nomad 15, its unique design gives 
the best mass/baseplate ratio available on the market and with a reduced 
environmental
footprint. In Marine, Sercel launched QuietSea, its new passive acoustic 
monitoring (PAM) system designed to detect the presence of marine mammals during
seismic operations which is set to revolutionize PAM within the seismic 
industry. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Equipment division EBITDAs</B> was $50 million, a margin of 26%. 
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Equipment division EBIT</B> was $39 million, a margin of 20%. The 
margin was impacted by lower revenue, by an unfavorable &#128;/$ exchange rate 
as in Q1
2014 and by pressure on prices. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Equipment division 
Capital Employed </B>was $0.8 billion at the end of June 2014. </P>

Roman" ALIGN="center">Page&nbsp;6 </P>

<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><B>&nbsp;</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right"><B>2.6</B></TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom"><B>&nbsp;&nbsp;</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><B>&nbsp;</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right"><B>2.4</B></TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom"><B>&nbsp;&nbsp;</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><B>&nbsp;</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right"><B>NA</B></TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom"><B>&nbsp;&nbsp;</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom"><B>&nbsp;</B></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" ALIGN="right"><B>NA</B></TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom"><B>&nbsp;&nbsp;</B></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman"><B>Acquisition division Total Revenue </B>was $481 
million, down 21% year-on-year and down 14% sequentially. In these
difficult market conditions, operational performance remained strong in marine 
with production rate at 92%. External revenue was $241 million. </P> <P 
STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Marine Acquisition </B>revenue was $407 
million, down 20% year-on-year and down 10% sequentially. 52% of the fleet was 
dedicated to multi-client programs. Utilization rate was at a high level this 
quarter for the
whole fleet with availability rate at 94% and a production rate at 92%. After 
the Symphony was decommissioned in February, we operated 17 3D vessels including
source vessels this quarter. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; 
font-family:Times New Roman">On the 19<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-
align:top">th</SUP> of June, CGG and Sovcomflot signed an agreement to form a 
joint venture
company dedicated to conducting high-end 3D marine seismic acquisition services.
The joint venture, to be called Arctic Geophysical Exploration (AGE), will be 
51% owned by Sovcomflot and 49% owned by CGG. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Land and Airborne Acquisition </B>revenue was 
$74 million, down 21% year-on-year and down 30% sequentially. This decrease is 
mainly due to weak market conditions across the regions. Revenue was low in 
Airborne due to
reduced mining activity and flat oil&nbsp;&amp; gas market. </TD></TR></TABLE> 
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Acquisition division EBITDAs</B> was $95 million, a margin of 20%.
</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Acquisition Division Operating Income</B> was at $19 million with 
an improvement in marine acquisition profitability sequentially. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Acquisition division EBIT</B> was $6 million a margin of 1% due to
the $(13) million negative contribution of the equity from investees (including 
40% of
the Seabed Geosolutions JV). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt;
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Acquisition division Capital 
Employed</B> was $2.4 billion at the end of June 2014. </P>

18% year-on-year and up 3% sequentially. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Multi-client revenue</B> was $128 million, down
36% year-on-year and stable sequentially in the context of overall lower 
exploration spending and delays in operations and permitting issues in Brazil.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-
bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><I>Prefunding revenue </I>was $92 million up 6% 
year-on-year and up 15% sequentially. Multi-client cash capex was 
$175&nbsp;million, 53% prefunded and mainly focused on our footprint extension 
in mature basins such as
the Norwegian North Sea (Horda) but also in the Gulf of Mexico with the 
continuation of our IBALT program. On the 15<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-
align:top">th</SUP> of May, CGG started acquiring a large BroadSeis<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">TM</SUP> 3D multi-client survey 
program in the deep and ultra-deep waters of the Espirito Santo Basin. The 
project has received high prefunding from major industry players. At the EAGE, 
CGG announced the
release of the Fast Trax<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">TM</SUP> 
processed data from its Deux multi-client IBALT survey covering 357 blocks in 
the Gulf of Mexico. The Fast Trax seismic images have been delivered on schedule
less than
seven months after completion of the survey. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-
size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><I>After-sales revenue</I> was $35 million, down 
68% year-on-year and down 26% sequentially. This fall is mainly due to our
clients&#146; reduction in spending on exploration and seismic activities. 
</TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-
size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Subsurface Imaging&nbsp;&amp; Reservoir 
</B>revenue was $172 million, up 2% year-on-year and 6% sequentially in line 
with our expectations. Demand for imaging, reservoir services and software 
remains strong.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt;
font-family:Times New Roman"><B>GGR Division EBITDAs</B> was $159 million, a 
margin of 53%. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>GGR Division EBIT</B> was $62 million, a margin of 21%. The multi-
client depreciation rate amounted to 62%, leading to a $1,012&nbsp;million Net 
Book Value
at the end of June 2014. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>GGR Division Capital 
Employed</B> was $2.9 billion at the end of June 2014. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Second Quarter 2014 Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Group Total Revenue</B> was $689 million, down 33% year-on-year 
and down 15% sequentially. This breaks down to 22% from the Equipment division, 
35% from the
Acquisition division, and 43% from the GGR division. </P> <P STYLE="font-
size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

New Roman"><B>First Half 2014 Financial Results </B></P>

New Roman"><B>Group Total Revenue </B>was $1.495 billion down 21% compared to 
2013 due to weakening market conditions. This breaks down to 21% from the 
Equipment
division, 40% from the Acquisition division and 39% from the GGR division. </P>

transactions in April to extend the average debt maturity periods from 4 to 
approximatively 6 years: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-

at 5.875%, the lowest rate ever obtained for a High Yield Bond issued by CGG, 
due 2020: </TD></TR></TABLE>

</TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><B>Net Debt to Equity Ratio: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; 
margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Group gross debt
was $2.960
billion at the end of June 2014. Available cash was $385 million and Group net 
debt was $2.575 billion. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; 
font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net debt to equity ratio, at the 
end of June
2014, was 75%. </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman"><B>About CGG </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-
bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>CGG
(www.cgg.com) is a fully integrated Geoscience company providing leading 
geological, geophysical and reservoir capabilities to its broad base of 
customers primarily from the global oil and gas industry. Through its three 
complementary business
divisions of Equipment, Acquisition and Geology, Geophysics&nbsp;&amp; Reservoir
(GGR), CGG brings value across all aspects of natural resource exploration and 
exploitation. </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times 
New Roman"><I>CGG employs over 9,500 people around the world, all with a Passion
for Geoscience and working together to deliver the best solutions to its 
customers.
</I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-
family:Times New Roman"><I>CGG is listed on the Euronext Paris SA (ISIN: 
0000120164) and the New York Stock Exchange (in the form of American Depositary 
Shares. NYSE: CGG).
